<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gebruken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gibrūkan</i>. Equivalent to modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bruiken</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebruiken.html>gebruiken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to use</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to consume, to eat or <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> (food or <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a>)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:consumeren.html>consumeren</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nuttigen.html>nuttigen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to consume (resources or goods)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:consumeren.html>consumeren</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbruiken.html>verbruiken</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:compliceren.html>compliceren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to complicate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, either from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">complicatie</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">complication</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or modeled on <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">compliquer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to complicate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, anyhow ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">complicare</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to complicate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gecompliceerd.html>gecompliceerd</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gecompliceerder.html>gecompliceerder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">gecompliceerdst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>complicated, complex or convoluted</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***gedaagde.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedaagde.html>gedaagde</a> (15960)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gedaagd.html>gedaagd</a></i>, the past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dagen.html>dagen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to summon (to court)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(session) day</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gedaagde.html>gedaagde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gedaagden.html>gedaagden</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A summoned person, be it a party, witness or other.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">gedagvaarde</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">opgeroepene</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (wider)</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***gedachtegoed.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedachtegoed.html>gedachtegoed</a> (93276)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gedachte.html>gedachte</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></i>, probably a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gedankengut</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gedachtegoed.html>gedachtegoed</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>body of thought, belief system, thinking, philosophy <span class="defdate">[from ca. 1930s]</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>Twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:broers.html>broers</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:raakten.html>raakten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bekend.html>bekend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gedachtegoed.html>gedachtegoed</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Schopenhauer. <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>moest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> hard <a href = vnd.unilang:lachen.html>lachen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pleegde.html>pleegde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zelfmoord.html>zelfmoord</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Two brothers once became familiar with Schoperhauer's <b>thought</b>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedicht.html>gedicht</a> (3563)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gedichte</i>. Equivalent to an <a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a> noun derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dichten.html>dichten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dictare</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:gedicht.html>Gedicht</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">gediht</i>.
</p>

***geding.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geding.html>geding</a> (23846)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gedinge</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ding.html>ding</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">matter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geding.html>geding</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geding.html>gedingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geding.html>gedingetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lawsuit</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Commonly used in the expression (Netherlands) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kort.html>kort</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geding.html>geding</a></i> ~ (Belgium) <i>kortgeding</i> ‘summary procedure’ (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:kort.html>kort</a></i> ‘short’).

***gedogen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedogen.html>gedogen</a> (47385)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gedogen.html>gedogen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gedōgen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gadaugijaną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">dogen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gedogen.html>gedogen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tolerate, to permit, to condone</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gedogen.html>gedogen</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:overgankelijk.html>overgankelijk</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:afzien.html>afzien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> bestraffende of ondermijnende <a href = vnd.unilang:maatregelen.html>maatregelen</a>
